<p class="has-text-align-left">GL Environment is a water treatment solutions and product supplier company. We have 16 years of application experience in the water treatment industry. </p>



<p class="has-text-align-left">Main supply products: dosing pump, diaphragm pump, water quality instrument, agitator, flow meter, pressure transmitter, solenoid valve, chemical pump, screw pump, water pump, filter press and dosing system. Main brands are ‘HAOSH‘, ‘AOBL‘ and ‘Apure‘. Apure brand mainly includes process control equipment: Water quality instrument, Flow meter, Level measuring instrument, Pressure&#8230;</p>
